portrait_groups = {
	draconid = {
		default = draconid_female_01
		game_setup = { #will run with a limited country scope. species and government is set but the country does not actually exist
			add = {
				trigger = {
					ruler = {
						OR = {
							gender = male
							gender = indeterminable
						}
					}
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_male_01
					draconid_male_02
					draconid_male_03
					draconid_male_04
				}
			}
			add = {
				trigger = {
					ruler = {
						OR = {
							gender = female
							gender = indeterminable
						}
					}
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_female_01
					draconid_female_02
					draconid_female_03
					draconid_female_04
				}
			}
			#set = {
			#	trigger = { ... }
			#	portraits = { ... }
			#	#using "set =" instead of "add" will first clear any portraits already added
			#}
		}		
		
		#species scope
		species = { #generic portrait for a species
			add = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { species = { species_gender = male } }
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_female_01
					draconid_female_02
					draconid_female_03
					draconid_female_04
				}
			}
			add = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { species = { species_gender = female } }
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_male_01
					draconid_male_02
					draconid_male_03
					draconid_male_04
				}
			}
		}		
		
		#pop scope
		pop = { #for a specific pop
			add = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { species = { species_gender = male } }
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_female_01
					draconid_female_02
					draconid_female_03
					draconid_female_04
				}
			}
			add = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { species = { species_gender = female } }
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_male_01
					draconid_male_02
					draconid_male_03
					draconid_male_04
				}
			}
		}
		
		#leader scope
		leader = { #scientists, generals, admirals, governor
			add = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						gender = female
						gender = indeterminable
					}
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_female_01
					draconid_female_02
					draconid_female_03
					draconid_female_04
				}
			}
			add = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						gender = male
						gender = indeterminable
					}
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_male_01
					draconid_male_02
					draconid_male_03
					draconid_male_04
				}
			}
		}

			
		#leader scope 
		ruler = {
			add = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						gender = female
						gender = indeterminable
					}
				}
				portraits = {
					draconid_female_01
